```

#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x3DC7 [0x42] SET_CLI_EVENT_CANCEL_DATA()
  1: 0x3DC8 [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x55AD)
  2: 0x3DCB [0x5D] SET_MUSIC_VOLUME(volume=0*, fade_time=300*)
  3: 0x3DD0 [0x46] CAMERA_CONTROL: Disable user control
  4: 0x3DD2 [0x38] SET_CLIENT_EVENT_MODE(mode=147*)
  5: 0x3DD5 [0x34] LOAD_UNLOAD_ZONE(zone_id=584*)
